queryT: SELECT `point` FROM `users` WHERE `user_id` = 2082435505 ORDER BY `point` DESC LIMIT 1
get_var: SELECT `point` FROM `users` WHERE `user_id` = 2082435505 ORDER BY `point` DESC LIMIT 1
queryT: 
        SELECT 
            u.user_id,
            u.name AS user_name,
            u.point,
            l.id AS league_id,
            l.icon AS league_icon,
            l.name AS league_name
        FROM users u
        LEFT JOIN league l ON l.point = (
            SELECT MAX(l2.point)
            FROM league l2
            WHERE l2.point <= u.point
        )
        ORDER BY u.point DESC
        LIMIT 10;
    
get_result: 
        SELECT 
            u.user_id,
            u.name AS user_name,
            u.point,
            l.id AS league_id,
            l.icon AS league_icon,
            l.name AS league_name
        FROM users u
        LEFT JOIN league l ON l.point = (
            SELECT MAX(l2.point)
            FROM league l2
            WHERE l2.point <= u.point
        )
        ORDER BY u.point DESC
        LIMIT 10;

queryT: SELECT `point` FROM `users` WHERE `user_id` = 2082435505 ORDER BY `point` DESC LIMIT 1
get_var: SELECT `point` FROM `users` WHERE `user_id` = 2082435505 ORDER BY `point` DESC LIMIT 1
queryT: 
        SELECT 
            u.user_id,
            u.name AS user_name,
            u.point,
            l.id AS league_id,
            l.icon AS league_icon,
            l.name AS league_name
        FROM users u
        LEFT JOIN league l ON l.point = (
            SELECT MAX(l2.point)
            FROM league l2
            WHERE l2.point <= u.point
        )
        ORDER BY u.point DESC
        LIMIT 10;
    
get_result: 
        SELECT 
            u.user_id,
            u.name AS user_name,
            u.point,
            l.id AS league_id,
            l.icon AS league_icon,
            l.name AS league_name
        FROM users u
        LEFT JOIN league l ON l.point = (
            SELECT MAX(l2.point)
            FROM league l2
            WHERE l2.point <= u.point
        )
        ORDER BY u.point DESC
        LIMIT 10;

queryT: SELECT `point` FROM `users` WHERE `user_id` = 2082435505 ORDER BY `point` DESC LIMIT 1
get_var: SELECT `point` FROM `users` WHERE `user_id` = 2082435505 ORDER BY `point` DESC LIMIT 1
queryT: 
        SELECT 
            u.user_id,
            u.name AS user_name,
            u.point,
            l.id AS league_id,
            l.icon AS league_icon,
            l.name AS league_name
        FROM users u
        LEFT JOIN league l ON l.point = (
            SELECT MAX(l2.point)
            FROM league l2
            WHERE l2.point <= u.point
        )
        ORDER BY u.point DESC
        LIMIT 10;
    
get_result: 
        SELECT 
            u.user_id,
            u.name AS user_name,
            u.point,
            l.id AS league_id,
            l.icon AS league_icon,
            l.name AS league_name
        FROM users u
        LEFT JOIN league l ON l.point = (
            SELECT MAX(l2.point)
            FROM league l2
            WHERE l2.point <= u.point
        )
        ORDER BY u.point DESC
        LIMIT 10;
